Monad_1 = Monad{
  baseMonoid = M_87
  pure 0 = Va 0
  join $ V                    = V
  join $ Va V                 = V
  join $ Va (Va 0)            = Va 0
  join $ Va (Vb 0)            = Vb 0
  join $ Va (Vc 0 1)          = Vc 0 1
  join $ Vb V                 = V
  join $ Vb (Va 0)            = Vb 0

  join $ Vb (Vc 0 1)          = V
  join $ Vc V V               = V
  join $ Vc V (Va 0)          = V
  join $ Vc V (Vb 0)          = V
  join $ Vc V (Vc 0 1)        = V
  join $ Vc (Va 0) V          = V
  join $ Vc (Va 0) (Va 1)     = Vc 0 1
  join $ Vc (Va 0) (Vb 1)     = V
  join $ Vc (Va 0) (Vc 1 2)   = V
  join $ Vc (Vb 0) V          = V
  join $ Vc (Vb 0) (Va 1)     = V
  join $ Vc (Vb 0) (Vb 1)     = V
  join $ Vc (Vb 0) (Vc 1 2)   = V
  join $ Vc (Vc 0 1) V        = V

  join $ Vc (Vc 0 1) (Vc 2 3) = V

  pure 0 = Va 0
  join $ V                    = V
  join $ Va V                 = V
  join $ Va (Va 0)            = Va 0
  join $ Va (Vb 0)            = Vb 0
  join $ Va (Vc 0 1)          = Vc 0 1
  join $ Vb V                 = V
  join $ Vb (Va 0)            = Vb 0
  join $ Vb (Vb 0)            = Vb 0
  join $ Vb (Vc 0 1)          = Vc 0 1
  join $ Vc V V               = V
  join $ Vc V (Va 0)          = V
  join $ Vc V (Vb 0)          = V
  join $ Vc V (Vc 0 1)        = V
  join $ Vc (Va 0) V          = Vc 0 0
  join $ Vc (Va 0) (Va 1)     = Vc 0 1
  join $ Vc (Va 0) (Vb 1)     = Vc 0 0
  join $ Vc (Va 0) (Vc 1 2)   = Vc 0 0
  join $ Vc (Vb 0) V          = Vc 0 0
  join $ Vc (Vb 0) (Va 1)     = Vc 0 1
  join $ Vc (Vb 0) (Vb 1)     = Vc 0 0
  join $ Vc (Vb 0) (Vc 1 2)   = Vc 0 0
  join $ Vc (Vc 0 1) V        = Vc 0 1
  join $ Vc (Vc 0 1) (Va 2)   = Vc 0 1
  join $ Vc (Vc 0 1) (Vb 2)   = Vc 0 1
  join $ Vc (Vc 0 1) (Vc 2 3) = Vc 0 1
}
